<UserId.>100859199451147660572< /UserId.><username>Sporty Encouragement</username>< date>
1604705712803< /date>
<Rate>5</Rate><Text>This place was found in spontaneity with my girlfriend and I looking for a quick and easy seafood restaurant. Little did I know what I got us into... Came in a me was seated indoors nearly immediately. This waved a red flag at me, walking in and being seated immediately?? I was a bit confused and yet curious to find out why it was so easy. Then it came down to order. I attempted to order something that was not on the menu. The server said that he can't put in an order of something that doesn't exist on the menu. I asked him to talk to the chefs and they made perfect sense as to why I ordered was not a possibility. Instead of denying me they treated me as if I was family! Not to stop there, the food was delicious and nutritious. Speaking of using the secret ingredient of (love) you can taste something beyond all tangible ingredients. <Pictures>None</Pictures><name>Colleen Wang<//name>< text>
I have gone to see Dr. Sabate several times. He seemed nice enough, even if a touch arrogant. He took over the practice when Dr. Hoag retired. I tried two other dentists in Redlands but since I hate all dental visits generally, trying different dentists was very stressful. Better the one you know ...

I liked that the practice does not use Latex.  I did not like that their rates were high. I liked the dental hygienist I tried. Her cleaning was the best I've ever had.  I likd his office staff.  His technical skill was ok but I found that 2 out of the 3 times he gave me blocks, my gums were bruised and tender.

He recommended I get my teeth whitened, which I had previously been told would not be very helpful. After spending the time and money to have them "whitened" I had only a very minimal improvement. Guess the other dentist was right. I wished I had questioned him more. He suggested I whiten again two visits later.

He told me I had a chip that needed repair and I ended up with a shorter front tooth. When I asked if that could be fixed he categorically said he didn't shorten it. However, when his own pictures of "before and after" were reviewed closely my tooth was indeed shorter. Eyeballing a photo is not always accurate. I will be having that repaired elsewhere.

I liked that he could fix a cavity, make and put in a crown in the same visit. I didn't like how much it hurt afterwards.<//text>
